<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">medicine</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">medicīna</i>.

***mee.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:mee.html>mee</a> (100)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From older <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:mede.html>mede</a></i> with the frequent loss of intervocalic <i>-d-</i> (cf. <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kou.html>kou</a></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:vs.html>vs</a>. <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:koude.html>koude</a></i> ["cold"]; <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:slee.html>slee</a></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:vs.html>vs</a>. <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:slede.html>slede</a></i> ["sleigh"]). The forms <i><a href = vnd.unilang:mee.html>mee</a></i> and <i><a href = vnd.unilang:mede.html>mede</a></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:were.html>were</a> subsequently distributed to different senses.
</p>

<li>along, together (i.e. with one)</li></ol>

<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:mee.html>mee</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">with</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:maken.html>maken</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to make</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">mēre</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">meri</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*<a href = vnd.unilang:mari.html>mari</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*móri</i>.

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">mêre</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*mēro</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*maizô</i>.

***meerkat.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:meerkat.html>meerkat</a> (103143)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">meercatte</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">monkey, ape</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*merikatta</i>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:meer.html>meer</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kat.html>kat</a></i>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Old High German">Old High German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="goh">merikazza</i> (<span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Meerkatze</i>).
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:meerkat.html>meerkat</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:meerkatten.html>meerkatten</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:meerkat.html>meerkatje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>A guenon, vervet, talapoin or patas; one of a number of <a href = vnd.unilang:monkeys.html>monkeys</a> of the genus <i>Cercopithecus</i>, or of the tribe <i>Cercopithecini</i>.
<ul><li><b>2013</b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:bas.html>Bas</a> Vlugt, <i>Namibië, Botswana <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> Zimbabwe</i>.
<dl><dd><a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>De</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:groene.html>groene</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:meerkat.html>meerkat</a></b> of <i>vervet monkey</i> (<i>Cercopithecus aethiops</i>) <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:meest.html>meest</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:voorkomende.html>voorkomende</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:aap.html>aap</a> in <a href = vnd.unilang:zuidelijk.html>zuidelijk</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:afrika.html>Afrika</a>.
<dl><dd>The <b>African green monkey</b> or <i>vervet monkey</i> (<i>Cercopithecus aethiops</i>) <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> the most common monkey in southern Africa.</dd></dl></dd></dl></li>
<li><b>2016</b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:sterre.html>Sterre</a> Leufkens, <i><a href = vnd.unilang:taal.html>Taal</a></i>, in <i><a href = vnd.unilang:elementaire.html>Elementaire</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:deeltjes.html>deeltjes</a></i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:vol.html>vol</a>. 40, Amsterdam University Press (publ.), page 32.
<dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>Het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:bijzonder.html>bijzondere</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:aan.html>aan</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:meerkatten.html>meerkatten</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dat.html>dat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ze.html>ze</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hun.html>hun</a> waarschuwingssignalen <a href = vnd.unilang:betekenisvol.html>betekenisvol</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:kunnen.html>kunnen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:combineren.html>combineren</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:met.html>met</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:andere.html>andere</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:woordjes.html>woordjes</a>.</span><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">The special thing about <b>guenons</b> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> that they can meaningfully combine their warning signals with other short <a href = vnd.unilang:words.html>words</a>.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ul></li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:meerkat.html>meerkat</a></b> <span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic">v</span>/<span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic">m</span> <sup id="cite_ref-3" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-3"> | 3 | </a></sup>
</p>
<ol><li>één <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:aantal.html>aantal</a> Afrikaanse apensoorten <a href = vnd.unilang:uit.html>uit</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> Cercopithecus-familie.</li></ol>

***meert.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:meert.html>meert</a> (64043)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Related to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:marter.html>marter</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/West_Frisian_language" class="extiw" title="w:West Frisian language">West Frisian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fy">murd</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:meert.html>meert</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:meert.html>meerten</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">Groningen<span class="ib-comma">,</span> dialectal</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en">polecat</span>
<ul><li><b>1914</b> February 2, "<a href = vnd.unilang:over.html>Over</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ons.html>ons</a> Dialect, XI.", <i>Nieuwsblad <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:noorden.html>Noorden</a></i>, second part.
<dl><dd><a href = vnd.unilang:zit.html>Zit</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> „<b><a href = vnd.unilang:meert.html>meert</a></b>” in <a href = vnd.unilang:benauwdheid.html>benauwdheid</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:dan.html>dan</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:stoot.html>stoot</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hij.html>hij</a> allerakeligste <a href = vnd.unilang:klanken.html>klanken</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:uit.html>uit</a>.</dd></dl></li>
<li><b>1929</b> March 16, "<a href = vnd.unilang:praatje.html>Praatjes</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:bij.html>bij</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:plaatjes.html>plaatjes</a>", <i>Nieuwsblad <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:noorden.html>Noorden</a></i>, third part.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:meesters.html>meesters</a> (8150)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

***meesterzet.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:meesterzet.html>meesterzet</a> (74425)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Compound of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:meester.html>meester</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:zet.html>zet</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:meesterzet.html>meesterzet</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:meesterzet.html>meesterzetten</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">board games</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A brilliant move.</li>

***meid.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:meid.html>meid</a> (700)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">meit</i>, variant of <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">meget</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*megith</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*magath</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*magaþs</i>. Compare also <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:maagd.html>maagd</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:meid.html>meid</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:meiden.html>meiden</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:meisje.html>meisje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:meiske.html>meiske</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:meidje.html>meidje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>girl, <a href = vnd.unilang:lass.html>lass</a>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>De</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:meiden.html>meiden</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:hadden.html>hadden</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:afgelopen.html>afgelopen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zaterdag.html>zaterdag</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> zwemwedstrijd.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">The <b><a href = vnd.unilang:girls.html>girls</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:had.html>had</a> a swimming match last Saturday.</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:goed.html>Goed</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:gedaan.html>gedaan</a>, <b><a href = vnd.unilang:meid.html>meid</a></b>!</i> ― <span class="e-translation">Well done, <b>girl</b>!</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>maid
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonyms:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bode.html>bode</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:deerne.html>deerne</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dienstbode.html>dienstbode</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dienstmaagd.html>dienstmaagd</a></span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="use-with-mention">Commonly used as an address for female <a href = vnd.unilang:pets.html>pets</a>, especially female dogs.</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:brave.html>Brave</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:meid.html>meid</a></b>!</i> ― <span class="e-translation">Good <b>girl</b>!</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li>Use in the singular may connote fortitude, bravery or acting like a grown-up, but it may also connote vulgarity or subservience due to the meaning “maid”. These connotations are much weaker in the plural, which can be used neutrally with little regard for context.</li>
<li>Use for <a href = vnd.unilang:adult.html>adult</a> women (and to a lesser degree for older adolescent <a href = vnd.unilang:girls.html>girls</a>) <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> often considered patronising, which <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> especially true of the diminutives.</li>
<li>The diminutive <i><a href = vnd.unilang:meidje.html>meidje</a></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> uncommon; the regular diminutive <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <i><a href = vnd.unilang:meisje.html>meisje</a></i> along with its variants <i><a href = vnd.unilang:meiske.html>meiske</a></i> and <i><a href = vnd.unilang:meisie.html>meisie</a></i>.</li></ul>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:meid.html>meid</a></b> <span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic">v</span>
</p>
<ol><li><span style="background-color:FFFFE0;font-style: italic;">(<a href = vnd.unilang:informeel.html>informeel</a>)</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:jonge.html>jonge</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:vrouw.html>vrouw</a>
<dl><dd><ul><li><i><a href = vnd.unilang:die.html>Die</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:meiden.html>meiden</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:hadden.html>hadden</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:weer.html>weer</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:eens.html>eens</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hoop.html>hoop</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:lol.html>lol</a>.</i> </li></ul></dd></dl></li>
<li><span style="background-color:FFFFE0;font-style: italic;">(<a href = vnd.unilang:verouderd.html>verouderd</a>)</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:werkster.html>werkster</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:dienstmeisje.html>dienstmeisje</a></li></ol>
<hr><h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Afgeleide_begrippen"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:afgeleide.html>Afgeleide</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:begrippen.html>begrippen</a></i></span></h5>
<ul><li>meidenband, meidenfilm, meidengek, meidengroep, meidenhuis, meidenmoeder, meidenopvanghuis, meidentelefoon, meidenverslinder, meidenverslindster, meidenwegloophuis</li></ul>
<div style="clear:both;"></div>
</body>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:meier.html>meier</a> (29198)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:meier.html>meier</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">head of the household personnel</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, which <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">māior</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">greater</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, short for <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">maior <a href = vnd.unilang:domus.html>domus</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">supervisor of a house</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.<sup id="cite_ref-1" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-1"> | 1 | </a></sup>
</p>

<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Yiddish" class="extiw" title="w:Yiddish">Yiddish</a></span> <i class="Hebr mention" lang="yi">מאה</i> |  <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="yi-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">méye</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Hebrew_language" class="extiw" title="w:Hebrew language">Hebrew</a></span> <i class="Hebr mention" lang="he">מֵאָה</i> |  <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="he-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn"><a href = vnd.unilang:me.html>me</a>'á</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">hundred</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Netherlands" class="extiw" title="w:Netherlands">Netherlands</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> informal</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <i><a href = vnd.unilang:honderdje.html>honderdje</a></i>, a 100 <a href = vnd.unilang:guilder.html>guilder</a> banknote, nowadays, however less frequently, used for a 100 euro banknote</li></ol>
